      FROM dp01a110 c

         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-06-30' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi

[2019/10/07 01:05:49] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-04-30' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-04-30' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-04-30' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-06-28' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-06-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-06-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/10/07 01:47:53] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-07-23' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-07-23' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-07-23' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-07-31' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO

          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi

         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-10-07' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-10-07' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-10-07' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;

[2019/10/07 04:07:38] SQL Query: SELECT CODIGO,NOMBRE FROM dp01a110 WHERE CODIGO_AUX = '38'
[2019/10/07 04:07:38] SQL Query: SELECT c.CODIGO, c.NOMBRE, activos.activo, pasivos.pasivo, capitales.capital
      FROM dp01a110 c 
      LEFT JOIN 
        (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS activo
         FROM dpmovimi 
         WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND ( CODMOV LIKE '1%' ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS activos ON activos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
        LEFT JOIN
          (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS pasivo
           FROM dpmovimi 
           WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '2%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS pasivos ON pasivos.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            LEFT JOIN
            (SELECT CODMOV, ID_EMPRESA, SUM(IMPORTE) AS capital
            FROM dpmovimi 
            WHERE FECHA_ASI <= '2019-02-28' AND (  CODMOV LIKE '3%'  ) AND ID_EMPRESA = 4 GROUP BY CODMOV) AS capitales ON capitales.CODMOV = c.CODIGO
            WHERE (c.CTAINACTIVA IS NULL OR c.CTAINACTIVA = 0) AND (  c.CODIGO LIKE '1%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '2%' OR c.CODIGO LIKE '3%'  ) ORDER BY c.CODIGO, activos.activo, capitales.capital;
